&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (b)&nbsp; an officer or employee_ _of
the Commonwealth, a State or a Territory,_ _appointed by the Minister to
be a prescribed authority;

is _prima facie _evidence of the matters stated in
the certificate.

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (3)&nbsp; In a prosecution for an offence against
this Act, an averment by the prosecutor in the information or complaint that
the defendant or any other person specified in the averment is identical with
the person specified in a certificate under this section is evidence of that
fact.

<a name="_Toc341190786"><span class="CharSectno">118</span>&nbsp;
Right of ministers of religion to receive fees</a>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Nothing in this Act affects the right of
a minister of religion who is an authorised celebrant to require or receive a
fee for or in respect of the solemnisation of a marriage.

<a name="_Toc341190787"><span class="CharSectno">120</span>&nbsp; Regulations</a>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The
Governor‑General may make regulations, not inconsistent with this Act,
prescribing all matters which by this Act are required or permitted to be
prescribed, or which are necessary or convenient to be prescribed for carrying
out or giving effect to this Act, and, in particular:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (a)&nbsp; prescribing the forms to be used
under this Act;

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (b)&nbsp; prescribing the practice and
procedure in relation to inquiries under Part&nbsp;II by a Judge or a
magistrate, including the summoning of witnesses, the production of documents,
the taking of evidence on oath or affirmation, the administering of oaths or
affirmations and the payment to witnesses of fees and of allowances for
expenses;

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (c)&nbsp; prescribing the manner of making
application for registration under Division&nbsp;1 of Part&nbsp;IV;

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (e)&nbsp; prescribing the conditions under
which, and the manner in which, marriages solemnised in accordance with the law
of an overseas country may be registered under section&nbsp;84;

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (f)&nbsp; making provision for the
recognition in Australia of marriages solemnised under a law in force in a
place outside Australia, being a law which makes provision appearing to the
Governor‑General to be similar to any provision made by Part&nbsp;V;

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (g)&nbsp; requiring the furnishing, to the
persons by whom registers of births are kept under a law of the Commonwealth or
a State or of any Territory, of information with respect to:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (i)&nbsp; legitimations effected
by sections&nbsp;89, 90 and 91; and

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (ii)&nbsp; orders made under
section&nbsp;92;

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (h)&nbsp; making provision for and in
relation to:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;(i)&nbsp; registration of
legitimations effected by sections&nbsp;89, 90 and 91 in cases where the births
of the legitimated children are not registered in any register of births kept
under a law of the Commonwealth or a State or of any Territory (including
provision requiring the furnishing of information); and

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (ii)&nbsp; the issue and effect
of certificates in respect of any such registration; and

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (j)&nbsp; prescribing penalties not
exceeding a fine of $200 for offences against the regulations. 

</div>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;">

</span>

<div class="Section4">

<a name="_Toc341190788"><span class="CharChapNo">The Schedule</span>—<span class="CharChapText">Persons whose consent is required to the marriage of a minor</span></a>

Section&nbsp;14&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 

<a name="_Toc341190789">Part&nbsp;I</a> 

_Where the Minor is not an
Adopted Child_

  of the minor by the order of a court </p>
  </td>
  <td width="186" valign="top" style="width:139.65pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt">
  <p class="subsection2" style="margin-left:0cm">The person or persons having the
  custody of the minor under the order of the court</p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td width="300" valign="top" style="width:225.15pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt">
  <p class="subsection2" style="margin-left:70.9pt;text-indent:-21.25pt">(iii)&nbsp; if
  the surviving parent is the father—</p>
  <p class="subsection2" style="margin-left:99.2pt;text-indent:-21.25pt">(A)&nbsp; if
  the minor lives permanently with the father</p>
  </td>
  <td width="186" valign="top" style="width:139.65pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt">
  <p class="subsection2" style="margin-top:4.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:
  0cm;margin-left:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid">

  The father </p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td width="300" valign="top" style="width:225.15pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt">
  <p class="subsection2" style="margin-left:99.2pt;text-indent:-21.25pt">(B)&nbsp; if
  the minor does not live permanently with the father and there is or are a
  guardian or guardians of the minor </p>
  </td>
  <td width="186" valign="top" style="width:139.65pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt">
  <p class="subsection2" style="margin-left:0cm;page-break-after:avoid">The
  guardian or guardians </p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td width="300" valign="top" style="width:225.15pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt">
  <p class="subsection2" style="margin-left:99.2pt;text-indent:-21.25pt">(C)&nbsp; if
  the minor does not live permanently with the father and there is no guardian
  of the minor </p>
  </td>
  <td width="186" valign="top" style="width:139.65pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt">

  page-break-after:avoid">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Where both parents of the minor are dead—</p>
  </td>
  <td width="186" valign="top" style="width:139.65pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt">

  </td>

1961 amended as indicated in the Tables below.

All relevant information pertaining to application, saving or
transitional provisions prior to 24&nbsp;November 2000 is not included in this <span style="layout-grid-mode:line">compilation</span>. For subsequent information _see_
Table A.

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;">

</span>

<div class="Section6">

_(a)_&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The _Marriage Act 1961 _was amended by
section&nbsp;3 only of the _Statute Law (Miscellaneous Provisions) Act 1988_,
subsection 2(1) of which provides as follows:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (1)&nbsp;&nbsp; Subject to this section, this Act
commences on the day on which it receives the Royal Assent.

_(b)_&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The _Marriage Act 1961 _was amended by section&nbsp;49
only of the _Law and Justice Legislation Amendment Act 1990_, subsection
2(1) of which provides as follows:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (1)&nbsp;&nbsp; Subject to this section, this Act
commences on the day on which it receives the Royal Assent.

_(c)_&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The _Marriage Act 1961 _was amended by Part&nbsp;3
(sections&nbsp;11–17) only of the _Sex Discrimination Act 1991_,
subsection 2(1) of which provides as follows:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (1)&nbsp;&nbsp; Part&nbsp;1, sections&nbsp;4, 7 and
8, Parts&nbsp;3 and 4 and the Schedule commence on 1&nbsp;August 1991.

_(d)_&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The _Marriage Act 1961 _was amended by
section&nbsp;24 only of the _Territories Law Reform Act 1992_, subsection
2(3) of which provides as follows:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (3)&nbsp;&nbsp; The remaining provisions of this Act
commence on 1&nbsp;July 1992.

_(e)_&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The _Marriage Act 1961 _was amended by
Schedule&nbsp;1 (Part&nbsp;7) by the _Family Law Reform (Consequential
Amendments) Act 1995_, subsection 2(4) of which provides as follows:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (4)&nbsp;&nbsp; The amendments made by Part&nbsp;7 of
Schedule&nbsp;1 commence on the commencement of section&nbsp;5 of the _Family
Law Reform Act 1995_.

_(f)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; _The _Marriage Act 1961 _was amended by
Schedule&nbsp;5 (item&nbsp;79) only of the _Statute Law Revision Act 1996_,
subsection 2(1) of which provides as follows:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (1)&nbsp;&nbsp; Subject to subsections&nbsp;(2) and
(3), this Act commences on the day on which it receives the Royal Assent.

_(g)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; _The_ Marriage Act 1961_ was amended by
Schedule&nbsp;13 only of the _Law and Justice Legislation Amendment Act 1999_,
subsection 2(1) of which provides as follows:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (1)&nbsp;&nbsp; Subject to this section, this Act
commences on the day on which it receives the Royal Assent.

_(h)_&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The _Marriage Act 1961 _was amended by
Schedule&nbsp;34 only of the _Law and Justice Legislation Amendment
(Application of Criminal Code) Act 2001_, subsection 2(1)(a) of which
provides as follows:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (1)&nbsp;&nbsp; Subject to this section, this Act
commences at the later of the following times:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (a)&nbsp;&nbsp; immediately after the
commencement of item&nbsp;15 of Schedule&nbsp;1 to the _Criminal Code
Amendment (Theft, Fraud, Bribery and Related Offences) Act 2000_;

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Item&nbsp;15 commenced on 24&nbsp;May 2001.

_(i)_&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Subsection 2(1) (items&nbsp;31 and 38) of
the _Statute Law Revision Act 2010_ provides as follows:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (1)&nbsp;&nbsp; Each
provision of this Act specified in column 1 of the table commences, or is taken
to have commenced, in accordance with column 2 of the table. Any other
statement in column 2 has effect according to its terms.

_(j)_&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Subsection
2(1) (items&nbsp;11 and 12) of the _Statute Law Revision Act 2011_
provides as follows:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (1)&nbsp;&nbsp; Each
provision of this Act specified in column 1 of the table commences, or is taken
to have commenced, in accordance with column 2 of the table. Any other statement
in column 2 has effect according to its terms.

<table class="MsoNormalTable" border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="474" style="margin-left:5.35pt;border-collapse:collapse">

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;">

</span>

<div class="Section8">

Table A

Application, saving or
transitional provisions

<span style="font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;">Criminal Code Amendment (Theft, Fraud, Bribery and
Related Offences) Act 2000</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;
font-style:normal"> (No.&nbsp;137, 2000)</span>

Schedule&nbsp;2

418&nbsp; Transitional—pre‑commencement
offences

(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Despite the amendment or
repeal of a provision by this Schedule, that provision continues to apply,
after the commencement of this item, in relation to:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (a)&nbsp; an
offence committed before the commencement of this item; or

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (b)&nbsp; proceedings
for an offence alleged to have been committed before the commencement of this
item; or

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (c)&nbsp; any
matter connected with, or arising out of, such proceedings;

as if the amendment or repeal had not
been made.

(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Subitem&nbsp;(1) does not
limit the operation of section&nbsp;8 of the _Acts Interpretation Act 1901_.

419&nbsp; Transitional—pre‑commencement
notices

If:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (a)&nbsp; a
provision in force immediately before the commencement of this item required
that a notice set out the effect of one or more other provisions; and

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (b)&nbsp; any or
all of those other provisions are repealed by this Schedule; and

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (c)&nbsp; the
first‑mentioned provision is amended by this Schedule;

the amendment of the first‑mentioned
provision by this Schedule does not affect the validity of such a notice that
was given before the commencement of this item.

<div style="border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 5.0pt 0cm;
margin-left:144.0pt;margin-right:144.0pt">

&nbsp;

</div>

<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;">Law
and Justice Legislation Amendment (Application of Criminal Code) Act 2001</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;font-style:normal"> (No.&nbsp;24,
2001)</span>

<a name="_Toc341190792"><span class="CharSectno">4</span>&nbsp;
Application of amendments</a>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (1)&nbsp; Subject to subsection&nbsp;(3), each amendment
made by this Act applies to acts and omissions that take place after the
amendment commences.

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (2)&nbsp; For the purposes of this section, if an
act or omission is alleged to have taken place between 2 dates, one before and
one on or after the day on which a particular amendment commences, the act or
omission is alleged to have taken place before the amendment commences.

<div style="border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 5.0pt 0cm;
margin-left:144.0pt;margin-right:144.0pt">

&nbsp;

</div>

<span style="font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;">Marriage Amendment Act 2002</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;font-style:normal"> (No.&nbsp;77,
2002)</span>

Schedule&nbsp;1

27&nbsp; Registration of existing marriage celebrants

(1)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; In this item:

**_existing marriage celebrant_** means a person:

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (a)&nbsp; in respect of whom an instrument
made under subsection 39(2) of the _Marriage Act 1961_ was in force
immediately before the commencement of item&nbsp;18 of this Schedule; and

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (b)&nbsp; who was not authorized by that
instrument to solemnize marriages as an officer of a State or Territory.

(2)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Each existing marriage celebrant is taken to have
been registered under Subdivision C of Division&nbsp;1 of Part&nbsp;IV of the _Marriage
Act 1961_ as a marriage celebrant on the date of the commencement of item&nbsp;18
of this Schedule.

(3)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; As soon as practicable after the commencement of
item&nbsp;18 of this Schedule, the Registrar of Marriage Celebrants must enter
in the register of marriage celebrants all details relating to the person that
are required by regulations made for the purposes of subsection 39D(5) to be
entered in the register in respect of a person who is registered as a marriage
celebrant.

Schedule&nbsp;2

5&nbsp; Application of items&nbsp;4 and 56

The amendments made by items&nbsp;4 and 56 apply in relation to
appointments of prescribed authorities made after those items commence.

10&nbsp; Application of item&nbsp;9

The amendment made by item&nbsp;9 applies in relation to notices
of intention to marry given after the item commences.

17&nbsp; Application of item&nbsp;16

The amendment made by item&nbsp;16 applies in relation to
Proclamations declared after the item commences.
